<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_913ab90e-1c21-40f3-be39-25a01d345cb1'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

All but the last book so far.
</span>
</div>
</div>

        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1030456153" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11643345980781003673"><b> 2.75-3 I didn't see any "misbehaving" stars </b><br/><br/><b> <i> "I knew that, without a doubt, I had just been ruined.â€ </i> </b><br/><br/>Before any of you attack me, Abbi Glines books are purely a guilty pleasure read for me. I may not rate them very high, but I do enjoy reading them. And I continue to read them because they are a nice little escape from reality and Ms. Glines writes some amazing angst. She just recycles her plots and uses too much instalove. I'm sorry, but I can't rate anything higher than that. It's a guilty </span>
  <span id="freeText11643345980781003673" style="display:none"><b> 2.75-3 I didn't see any "misbehaving" stars </b><br><br><b> <i> "I knew that, without a doubt, I had just been ruined.â€ </i> </b><br><br>Before any of you attack me, Abbi Glines books are purely a guilty pleasure read for me. I may not rate them very high, but I do enjoy reading them. And I continue to read them because they are a nice little escape from reality and Ms. Glines writes some amazing angst. She just recycles her plots and uses too much instalove. I'm sorry, but I can't rate anything higher than that. It's a guilty pleasure read y'all! <br><br>Anyways, Misbehaving is the story of "bad girl" Jess and Jason, the rock stars brother. From the moment the two of them meet, it's love. No really, I'm not joking. The plot went: they meet, they have one date, and on that first date they had sex. And after they have sex, Jason thinks this:<br><br><b> <i> "At some point she'd become my sole reason for breathing." </i> </b><br><br>Me at this point:<br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/untitled1.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1408574128i/10868099.png" alt=" photo untitled1.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>AND THIS WAS AFTER HER PUTTING OUT ON THE FIRST DATE!! (Great lesson there, I'll be sure to take notes). <br><br><b> <i> â€œI could tell she was one of those ridiculously gorgeous southern blondes. It was like the South had some special ingredient to raise them like that down here.â€ </i> </b><br><br>Anyways, neither one of the two MC's are really equipped for a real relationship, so they mess up quite a bit along the way. Like, really mess up. But it was entertaining to me.<br><br>I'm also not a huge fan of the Cinderella story, so a rich man soaring in and saving the day with his dick and money don't really do it for me. Oh well, on to the next one!<br><br><br><br></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2096543455" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2224935435418281668">This is the 6th book in this series I've been reading and I like most of the characters in all the books. This book was needed for a challenge and I new I could get it read in one sitting so I picked it up for that purpose. I like this series but I'm still a little tired of romance books. I did like this one better then the last book I read. At least this one didn't annoy me until around chapter 20.<br/><br/>I hate that for 2 or 3 chapters we have to deal with adults not talking to each other because in r</span>
  <span id="freeText2224935435418281668" style="display:none">This is the 6th book in this series I've been reading and I like most of the characters in all the books. This book was needed for a challenge and I new I could get it read in one sitting so I picked it up for that purpose. I like this series but I'm still a little tired of romance books. I did like this one better then the last book I read. At least this one didn't annoy me until around chapter 20.<br /><br />I hate that for 2 or 3 chapters we have to deal with adults not talking to each other because in real life people talk. There was a phone call and a woman answered. It wouldn't take 3 days to a week for a woman in real life to address that situation. It gets so annoying that a lot of these romance books do this. I understand it happening in YA (I kind of understand it happening) but for adults to act like a pack of teenagers drives me bat shit crazy.<br /><br />This story was about Jess who in the past books had hit on Marcus and then again on Cage. So of course in this books she was labeled the wild one or the girl who was trouble. In the past books we were not meant to like her so when I read this was about her I was not so excited to read about her BUT the guy who fell for her I just happen to like from the past books. Jason Stone is a good guy and the brother of rock star and the male MC in the first book of this series Jax Stone. It was fun to read about Jason. I did end up liking Jess by the end of this book but again I hate when they don't handle business and it drags on for 3 chapters. I loved the way it ended in that Jason ended up being her white knight. For Jess and her mother. It was very sweet.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />The one predictable part of this book was the way they went on and on about Jess's mom being a stripper and she never wants Jess to be in that line of work. It was said so many times you just knew that at some point Jess was in fact going to have to strip for some reason. I wasn't surprised when she interviewed and got a job stripping. <br /><br />The series as a whole is pretty good. All the books are super fast reading books and the content is cute. I have read 6 out of the 9 books so I know most of the characters and most of them I really like. It is fun to see how each progress with each book. One is married and has a baby now. Another of the characters are still together and they have a baby too. Not sure if they married or not yet. I recommend the books just know they are gripping by any means. Just fluffy cute books to pass the time away. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_667257270" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/667257270" />
    <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie"><img alt="Natasha is a Book Junkie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585046882p2/9389992.jpg" /></a>

        <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natasha is a Book Junkie" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie">Natasha is a Book Junkie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=natasha">natasha</a>,

          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer667257270" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6935962059598989978"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>â€œIâ€™ve always wanted a man to love me for me.â€</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>Just when I thought that after five instalments in the Sea Breeze series I would be safe in knowing what to expect in this book, I realised that you never know what youâ€™re going to get in an Abbi Glines novel. So very different from its prequels, this story is a gut-wrenching joy-ride beginning to end, with so many moments that will take your breath away with the intensity of emotions running through you. Jess is a bad girl that I adored, </span>
  <span id="freeText6935962059598989978" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>â€œIâ€™ve always wanted a man to love me for me.â€</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>Just when I thought that after five instalments in the Sea Breeze series I would be safe in knowing what to expect in this book, I realised that you never know what youâ€™re going to get in an Abbi Glines novel. So very different from its prequels, this story is a gut-wrenching joy-ride beginning to end, with so many moments that will take your breath away with the intensity of emotions running through you. Jess is a bad girl that I adored, her every action making me love her even more, and this is truly her book.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>â€œHe was a fairy tale. And I didnâ€™t live in a storybook.â€</i>
</blockquote><br>As someone who always saw herself as a bad girl from the wrong side of the tracks, Jess was raised to believe that her only way out from the life her mother had no choice but to live was by finding a man who would take care of her and save her from her reality. The only child of a single mother who could only make ends meet by working as a stripper, she never had a positive male role model around to make her believe that a good man is anything more than a fairy tale. Every man in her life used her for one thing and one thing alone, and she quickly learned that no man would ever offer her anything without expecting something in return. She was used to men putting her down, cheating on her, mistreating and disrespecting her, finding it very difficult to accept attentiveness with no strings attached.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>â€œEnjoy him, baby girl, but remember heâ€™s just a man. Heâ€™ll marry a girl with a trust fund. Watch your heart.â€</i>
</blockquote><br>When she meets Jason, she is immediately attracted to him physically, but the more time they spend together, the more she believes him to be completely out of her league. She doesnâ€™t even allow herself to daydream of a future with him, knowing guys like Jason never end up with girls like her. As their attraction grows and stems into a casual but very steamy affair between them, for the first time in her life, Jess learns what it feels like to be treated by a man with respect.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>â€œJess, if guys donâ€™t open doors for you, then they arenâ€™t worth your time.â€</i>
</blockquote><br>She finds Jasonâ€™s thoughtfulness and genuine interest in her as a person, not just her body, hard to accept at times. He makes her feel special, cared for, and soon her feelings towards him inevitably turn into a lot more than she knows she should feel. But she never stops believing that what they have is not permanent, expecting him to walk out of her life the moment he does not need her as a distraction any longer.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>â€œCould you get closure on something like this? Loving a man who didnâ€™t love you back?â€</i>
</blockquote><br>Jason never expected that a firecracker like Jess would finally be his undoing. As the younger brother of a rockstar, Jason has lived under that shadow all his life, never really knowing whether people liked him for him or because of his connection to a celebrity. He works hard to pave his own future, still unsure of what that future would be, but determined to become his own man and not always be known as someoneâ€™s brother. Jess shakes his picture-perfect life the moment she steps in front of his car with a baseball bat in her hand. He is drawn to her carefree spirit, her innate sex-appeal and the vulnerability she so desperately tries to hide. She acts like other peopleâ€™s treatment of her does not affect her, her sassiness being her shield against hurt, but Jason sees that underneath that bravado is an insecure young woman whose only wish is to be someoneâ€™s first choice, for someone other than her mother to finally put her first and make her feel safe. As much as he cannot stay away from her and finds himself feeling protective and possessive of her, he sees commitment being a complication he believes not to have time for at this stage in his life. He wants her, but he wonâ€™t allow himself to claim her completely, as he cannot see her fitting in his world.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>â€œI know this is just a little fling. Iâ€™m not expecting more.â€</i>
</blockquote><br>This is in so many ways a heartbreaking love story between a young woman who is willing to settle for less from the man she loves if it means she would have him in her life at all, and a young man still trying to find himself and slowly learning that the best things in life are always a little bit complicated. Jess is a heroine who made me want to beat up every man that had ever wronged her and whose kind heart and vulnerability were the highlights of the story for me. It took me some time to grow attached to Jason, his indecision when it came to claiming Jess as his own making me see red at times, but the vast difference in the way they were raised justified that in my eyes. This was a story whose heart-wrenching moments will stay with you, make you want to re-read them, re-live them. Nothing gets to me like scenarios of unrequited love, real or apparent, and this book got to me page after page, scene after scene. An absolute game changer in a series that keeps getting better and better.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>â€œAs the music played over the speakers and the waterfall in the pool filled the silence around us, I knew that without a doubt I had just been ruined.â€</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380382869i/740934.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://www.natashaisabookjunkie.com/2013/12/17/misbehaving-abbi-glines/" rel="nofollow noopener">See this review on my blog!</a> | <a href="http://www.facebook.com/natashaisabookjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Facebook!</a> | <a href="http://www.twitter.com/natashabkjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Twitter!</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9078845707120246870"> Before I start bashing this book in my review, I just want to say that Abbi Glines is a mastermind when it comes to emotional, gut-wrenching storylines. She knows exactly how to play with out hearts while making us feel all those wonderful, heartwarming feels, but every author can't have the perfect score in books and Misbehaving was apparently my least favorite work by Abbi.<br/><br/> You know when a book is so bad that it's actually hilarious. That's Misbehaving right there! At first I was frustrated w</span>
  <span id="freeText9078845707120246870" style="display:none"> Before I start bashing this book in my review, I just want to say that Abbi Glines is a mastermind when it comes to emotional, gut-wrenching storylines. She knows exactly how to play with out hearts while making us feel all those wonderful, heartwarming feels, but every author can't have the perfect score in books and Misbehaving was apparently my least favorite work by Abbi.<br /><br /> You know when a book is so bad that it's actually hilarious. That's Misbehaving right there! At first I was frustrated with the characters and their stupefied thoughts, but then I started noticing the cheesy dialogues that no one in there right mindset would ever say aloud, and this book became sort of entertaining. In a very bad way! I've never disliked an Abbi Glines book this much, there was a point around 21% where I straightaway wanted to DNF the story, but I'm very loyal to the author, hence the skimming! <br /><br />More to come...</span>

  <span id="freeText8181382445546352607" style="display:none">Title: Misbehaving<br />Series: Sea Breeze #6<br />Author: Abbi Glines<br />Genre: Contemporary Romance<br />Pages: 362<br />Heat Level: 3 out of 4 flames<br />Overall Star Rating: 4 out of 5 stars<br />Reviewed by Naughty Book Snitch Kay<br /><br />Ok, I admit it. I wasn't that excited to read about Jason Stone. Not that I didn't like the peeks we got of him earlier in this series, I just wasn't sure what to think of him.<br /><br />Well, I'm so glad I did read because it was so good. I loved both of the main characters. Jason was what a man should be. He was kind, caring, a little assholish and an alpha male when he had to be. Jess was a very sweet character. Misunderstood, underestimated and unsure of her true worth. She knew how to work a man. She's relied on her physical appearance for most of her life. <br /><br />Abbi Glines did a great job of bringing two totally different characters together. She made it a great adventure for Jess. It was touching, sweet and very sexy. Abbi Glines is a true master at her craft.<br /></span>

<div id="review_2211050569" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2211050569" />
    <a title="Natalia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52662522-natalia"><img alt="Natalia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485879776p2/52662522.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2211050569?book_show_action=true">Dec 11, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natalia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natalia" href="/user/show/52662522-natalia">Natalia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52662522-natalia?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52662522-natalia?shelf=newadult">newadult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2211050569" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3777080369467310596">This book was a bit of a disappointment for me. I mean I know that I'm reading an Abbi Glines book so I don't have really high expectations, but it's still my least favorite from the Sea Breeze series.<br/>This books follows Jess and Jason. Jason is Jax's brother. Jess doesn't have a wonderful life quite the opposite actually. And one day after beating her cheating ex boyfriends car she meets Jason. He helps her escape. If this seems a bit weird it was.<br/>Jess wasn't exactly the typical female character</span>
  <span id="freeText3777080369467310596" style="display:none">This book was a bit of a disappointment for me. I mean I know that I'm reading an Abbi Glines book so I don't have really high expectations, but it's still my least favorite from the Sea Breeze series.<br />This books follows Jess and Jason. Jason is Jax's brother. Jess doesn't have a wonderful life quite the opposite actually. And one day after beating her cheating ex boyfriends car she meets Jason. He helps her escape. If this seems a bit weird it was.<br />Jess wasn't exactly the typical female character. She was actually confident in her self and didn't depend on her boyfriend all of the time. However I didn't like Jason like at aÄºl. He was one of the worst male characters I've read before.<br />I really liked the Gilmore girls references. I'm a huge Gilmore girls fan so I loved them.<br />I really didn't like her mother and the overall message she sent. When she got sick Jess started working as a stripper to pay the bills. And her mother proposed this! Just No! It was as if her mother thought that for a girl to earn money and be successful she eighter had to be a stripper or marry someone rich. That's a horrible message to sent to a young girl and I totally disagree.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3777080369467310596" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nG+R1OTlR1Vu02TAr7mTZBeYM3K6nSOhXd3LSyOhycEN0U7q35FRlUYvLJK8p4FPXNe76eiEwlbFELhnQMpGpw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('P/wrio3jKd1blFwjmec197dr37c5E+dZlLsi8Mu64UCuQvS0tpc/HXNoFHGK+Sfc/CRXLGsKBq4MdlHcqNFuJg==')})
  }
